class=\"heading fradmcn\">A Brief History of Binary Options</div>\n\t<div class=\"aboutContent inner_ct\"><p>Binary options were popularized after the 2008 global financial crisis. This form of financial trading is particularly attractive to market participants who are interested in any of the 4 categories of investing: Commodities, Equities, Shares and Currencies. However, in binary options trading  <em>as the name suggests</em>  there are just 2 potential outcomes: Youre either in the money or youre out of the money. Binary options trading is akin to wagering at a casino, however your options are more favourable since you have a 50-50 chance of making the right decision. You are tasked with deciding whether the price of the underlying asset will increase or decrease by the time of expiry of the option. Binary options allow for self-regulation in the financial markets and they are also ideally suited to balancing out equities by way of speculation that the companys stock will decrease in value if it is overvalued, or increase in value if it is undervalued.</p>\n</div>\n\t</section>\t        \t        \t<section class=\"center-block clearfix\" id=\"top-section\">\n\t<div class=\"heading fradmcn\">Learn to Trade Binary Options Just Like the Pros!</div>\n\t<div class=\"aboutContent inner_ct\"><p>New or Inexperienced at Trading Binary Options?<br>\nLet experienced, winning traders share secrets that only experts know.<br>\n<a href=\"http://www.toptenbinarybrokers.com/ebook/\"><img class=\"wp-image-9333 alignright\" src=\"http://www.toptenbinarybrokers.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/ebook_242x390-186x300-186x300.png\" alt=\"ebook_242x390-186x300\" width=\"120\" height=\"194\"></a><br>\nFind out how to choose a legitimate broker,<br>\nthe tools you need to succeed when trading and&nbsp;strategies every pro trader swears by.<br>\nMaximize your chances of success and start winning trades.</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://www.toptenbinarybrokers.com/ebook/\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-9327 size-full\" src=\"http://www.toptenbinarybrokers.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/1.jpg\" alt=\"1\" width=\"271\" height=\"32\"></a></p>\n</div>\n\t</section>\t        \t        \t<section class=\"center-block clearfix\" id=\"top-section\">\n\t<div class=\"heading fradmcn\">So What Are Binary Options?</div>\n\t<div class=\"aboutContent inner_ct\"><p>In essence, binary options trading is all about speculating about the future price movement of an underlying asset. The price of that asset will either increase at the time of expiry or decrease at the time of expiry. If you are correct in your assessment, you will be <em>in the money</em>, and if you are incorrect in your assessment you will be <em>out of the money</em>. As such, all of your risks are known from the outset, and all of your potential profits are known up front too. Before you even make a trade you are fully apprised of the risks and the benefits of placing a <em>call</em> or <em>put</em> option. Additionally, binary options trading gives you the perfect opportunity to enter the financial markets with very little money down. And you do not need to place large bets on any underlying assets as you would in pure forex trading or stocks trading. At TopTenBinaryBrokers.com we will introduce you to the most cost-effective binary options trading platforms on the planet. You will gain a thorough understanding of these markets and the way they function.</p>\n</div>\n\t</section>\t        \t        \t<section class=\"center-block clearfix\" id=\"top-section\">\n\t<div class=\"heading fradmcn\">Who We Are  TopTenBinaryBrokers</div>\n\t<div class=\"aboutContent inner_ct\"><p>Here at TopTenBinaryBrokers we endeavour to provide you with pertinent and useful trading information relating to binary options trading. Are you aware that binary options trading has the potential generate profits in the region of 65-91%? That being said, please be advised that traders can also lose their entire investment.&nbsp;This is why binary options trading has taken off in the UK, Europe and indeed around the world. Perhaps the most impressive aspect of generating profits in the region of 65%  91% is the timeframe within which you can do it. Youre actually able to generate massive profits in as little as 1 minute.&nbsp;However, because these trades are binary, please be advised you can just as easily lose your investment in as little as 1 minute. Investors and traders rarely see such high returns on equity in any financial assets and any trader should be aware that trading binary options can be risky and might lead to the loss of the total investment.</p>\n<p>It is important however to understand that you never take physical possession of the assets that youre trading; youre simply speculating on the future price movement of the underlying asset. By forecasting price movements, you are essentially taking a position and a caveat is that the trade can go in your favor or against you. Should your prediction prove correct, you will end in the money. Unlike stocks trading and Forex trading, the actual size of the price movement is irrelevant &nbsp;<em>only the direction matters</em>. Other added benefits include the fact that there are no fees, commissions or hidden costs involved in trading binary options. You make the trade and you collect your profits. However, often times if you lose on your binary trade, the company you made the trade on will profit.</p>\n</div>\n\t</section>\t        \t        \t<section class=\"center-block clearfix\" id=\"top-section\">\n\t<div class=\"heading fradmcn\">How to Select the Right Broker</div>\n\t<div class=\"aboutContent inner_ct\"><p>Your success as a trader is largely dependent on the trading platform you select from the get-go. One such service available to you as a binary options trader is known as a <em>trading signal</em>. Consider for a moment that you may have multiple trades on the go simultaneously. It can become a little confusing, if not overwhelming to follow each of these trades in real time. This becomes especially important when the number of trades increases and the funds that you have invested in those trades increases. Trading signals allow you to receive automatic updates about important market information, and therefore allow you to track your binary options trades with greater precision.</p>\n<p>It should be stressed from the outset that no technology is fool-proof. Trading signals are only as good as the algorithms used to create them, which in turn are fully dependent on the people that designed them. There are many inherent benefits to using trading signals, however and these relate to their ability to notify you via SMS of important economic updates, price movements and related information. Specialised trading signal services claim to offer returns of approximately 70% or more and these can prove highly useful when you need instant updates wherever you are. Investors have been using trading signals software for quite some time now, and the efficacy of them really depends on the source, reliability and accuracy of the software provider.
